 (define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)

(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

Parsed df and pf: 
 (define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)

    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem explore-problem)
  (:domain explore-domain)
  (:objects
    kitchen laundry-room backyard living-room unknown-west street driveway unknown-north-backyard corridor bathroom bedroom - location
    north east west south - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at bathroom)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (visited backyard)
    (visited living-room)
    (visited bathroom)
    (door kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door laundry-room kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen laundry-room north)
    (door-open laundry-room kitchen south)
    (door kitchen backyard east)
    (door backyard kitchen west)
    (door-open kitchen backyard east)
    (door-open backyard kitchen west)
    (door kitchen unknown-west west)
    (door-closed kitchen unknown-west west)
    (door backyard unknown-north-backyard north)
    (door-closed backyard unknown-north-backyard north)
    (door backyard street south)
    (door backyard driveway east)
    (door backyard living-room north)
    (door living-room backyard south)
    (door-open backyard living-room north)
    (door-open living-room backyard south)
    (door living-room unknown-north-backyard north)
    (door-open living-room unknown-north-backyard north)
    (door living-room corridor east)
    (door living-room bathroom north)
    (door bathroom living-room south)
    (door-open living-room bathroom north)
    (door-open bathroom living-room south)
    (door bathroom bedroom east)
  )
  (:goal
    (or (and (not (visited unknown-west)) (at unknown-west))
        (and (not (visited street)) (at street))
        (and (not (visited driveway)) (at driveway))
        (and (not (visited unknown-north-backyard)) (at unknown-north-backyard))
        (and (not (visited corridor)) (at corridor))
        (and (not (visited bedroom)) (at bedroom)))
  )
)

  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
  )
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to ?dir))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain explore-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-closed ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )
  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (at ?loc1))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir)))
